First Special District Rent Reduction Meeting Yesterday Opened Fair Revival Rent Reduction Meeting; At the Same Time Held Rent Reduction Movement Week Opening Ceremony; Issued Declaration Demanding Landlords Voluntarily Reduce Rents 88

The Shanghai First Special District Rent Reduction Committee held a Fair Revival Rent Reduction Movement Assembly at the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Association at 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon, and held the Rent Reduction Movement Week opening ceremony. More than 5,000 representatives from all walks of life and citizens attended. It was resolved to reorganize the rent reduction branches of various lanes and roads, take consistent action, and petition landlords to voluntarily reduce rents, etc. A declaration calling for rent reduction was also issued. The details are as follows:

Grand Opening Announcement

Yesterday afternoon, around 1:00 PM, representatives from all walks of life had been arriving at the Ningbo Fellow Association on Tibet Road. By 2:00 PM, the number of attendees had increased even more enthusiastically. By 3:00 PM, it was extremely crowded, with an estimated attendance of over 5,000 people. The meeting place was the auditorium on the second floor of the Ningbo Fellow Association. Above the door hung a white cloth banner that read "Shanghai First Special District Rent Reduction Committee Rent Reduction Movement Assembly." The image of Sun Yat-sen was hung high on the stage, with the flags of the party and the nation crossed on the left and right. Around the meeting place were pasted rent reduction slogans with sharp words and profound meanings. There were also Hua Cheng Public School Boy Scouts maintaining order. At exactly 2:00 PM, the bell rang to open the meeting. After the Hua Cheng Public School Boy Scouts held the opening ceremony, the presidium members Li Aokui, Wang Jingdong, Sun Wenyi, Chen Jiufeng, and Wang Hesong successively took their seats. The master of ceremonies was Zhu Zhichun, and the stenographer was Zheng Dongshan. After Li Aokui led everyone in performing the ceremonial rites, he began the report, passing resolutions, and ending with entertainment. The meeting adjourned around 6:00 PM.

Chairman's Report

Chairman Wang Jingdong of the presidium reported the purpose of the meeting, stating briefly: "Today is the first day of Rent Reduction Movement Week. Holding the Fair Revival Rent Reduction Movement Assembly here aims to make great efforts in public awareness, with the goal of awakening landlords to voluntarily reduce rents. The number of attendees today is very enthusiastic, which shows that people earnestly hope that rent reduction will be implemented as soon as possible." Then Li Aokui gave a speech, saying that the rent reduction movement in this city has been noisy for a year, but due to environmental factors, it has not achieved its goal. Now, all industries are depressed, and countless people are unemployed. Those who pay attention to society now see that the market is extremely serious. If we do not find a way to remedy it, I am afraid that it will not only be the bankruptcy of industry and commerce. Reducing rent is not a thorough solution to the social economy, but implementing it in Shanghai at present can be said to be an effective golden needle to adjust the social economy and ensure social order and security. Therefore, we are carrying out rent reduction movement work. Comrades, please take the purpose of common survival and common prosperity to strongly request the landlords to implement it.

Report on Work

Then Chen Jiufeng reported on the guidance process for attending various district branches, stating briefly: "Most of the rent reduction branches have been established in the entire district, but there are still many lanes and roads that have not been organized. We should jointly establish rent reduction associations and petition landlords to implement rent reduction, so as to adjust finance and revive the economy." Next, Zhang Xianfang reported, briefly stating, "The rent reduction movement has been going on for a year, but because it has not achieved a unified goal, we are holding Rent Reduction Movement Week to commemorate and encourage the progress of the work." Later, Luo Zheng, Zheng Dongshan, Zhou Fuzhang, Zhu Baoluo, Zheng Xiaolin, and others successively reported on rent reduction work, with the general meaning being that today's meeting aims to promote unified rent reduction, and also commemorate the success of part of the rent reduction movement over the past year. Therefore, after the committee's resolution, from today until the end of the month, it will be named Rent Reduction Movement Week and handled by the Propaganda Department. We rely on the public opinion circles and all walks of life to make consistent sympathetic claims, petition landlords, and think of the friendship of sharing the same boat, so that the expression of voluntary rent reduction can be achieved. The rent reduction committee has never had funds to cover expenses. This time, we need to print paper, distribute slogans and leaflets, and produce special publications, so we are distributing tickets at the entrance, collecting a small amount of printing paper fees, 20 cents per ticket, to show support. We do not donate money outside. This work is nothing more than a public movement. Rent reduction work requires the concerted efforts of everyone to maintain unity and a consistent spirit. Today's entertainment is not for eye-catching or hearing pleasure, but for the consistent promotion of rent reduction, which is closely related to our own interests and the important task of relieving our own burdens.

Passing Proposals

Yesterday's assembly passed the following proposals: (1) Resolving the problem of relieving the suffering of the people, and petitioning the landlords to reduce rents through common unity, the resolution was passed. (2) Requesting the party and government authorities to consult with the landlord associations to decide on rent reduction methods, the resolution was passed. (3) Sending a letter to the Public Works Department to re-evaluate the land price, so as to match the rent price, the resolution was passed. (4) All lanes and roads should uniformly form rent reduction branches, to emphasize unity, the resolution was passed. (A) Letters should be sent to the organizations of all sectors. (B) Organizations of branch associations must come to the meeting to register. (C) Already established branch associations must re-register to make the system clear. (5) Issuing a declaration calling for rent reduction, read by Sun Wenyi, the resolution was passed.

Calling for Rent Reduction

Yesterday, the assembly issued a declaration calling for rent reduction, which stated: "Even ants are greedy for life, who would want to die without clothes and freezing to death, or starving to death? Although it is not what they want, they have no choice. Being oppressed by rent and affecting food and clothing, resulting in death, is also a matter of no choice? Moreover, food and clothing can sometimes be reasonably self-controlled, but in the item of housing, there is no freedom to expand or contract. Rain, snow, wind, and frost are sheltered by houses, and cooking, washing, and drying cannot be done without houses. Especially the birth, old age, sickness, and death of family members, and personnel arrangements, none of which can do without houses. Among the 3.5 million residents of this city, excluding those who own their own houses and those who sleep on the streets, those who rent houses account for 80 or 90 percent. In recent years, the market has been declining and unemployment has been increasing. Most people have already moved from large houses to small houses, and from Tonglou Tongxiang to Tingzizao Pi or two- or three-story lofts. Who knows that the degree of recession is even worse than before? At this time of economic hardship, even living in the smallest house that cannot be shrunk is not enough to compensate for the rent price without saving clothes and reducing food. If even food and clothing are not enough, how can one live? Prostitution and theft are emerging one after another, and suicides are happening every day. The so-called prosperity of the market and the so-called maintenance of people's livelihood are truly nothing more than myths. Even the general price of goods has been declining one after another, but only the item of rent has not seen any change so far. Those who have responsibility are indifferent and those who can muddle through are all muddling through. It is not a misfortune that Shanghai, the only metropolis in our country, has such unfair things! The people of this association are deeply afraid that the collapse of the whole people will be even worse for the commercial market to go bankrupt without end. We should make preparations before it rains, and specially carry out the work of the Fair Revival and rent reduction movement, in order to seek remedy and stabilize society. I hope you will all see this. The Shanghai First Special District Fair Revival and Rent Reduction Movement Assembly."

Radio Broadcasting

Yesterday, each radio station broadcasted messages, requesting landlords to reduce rents. A reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency recorded the original text as follows: "In order to revive and prosper the Shanghai market, in order to consider the burden of tenants, we hope that real estate owners will reduce rents, not to take advantage of the situation. This is something that was publicized for a while last year, and was negotiated several times, but in the end it did not achieve the purpose we hoped for. A meaningful and reasonable thing suddenly stopped invisibly, and died out silently. On the tenant side, doubts arose and it was unclear why. On the real estate owner side, they thought it was a fantasy and a joke. In fact, this is very obvious. On the one hand, it is because the citizens still have a solid unity and self-improvement, and on the other hand, it is because the real estate owners still do not understand the reason why rent reduction is necessary, are ignorant of the times, and want to maintain face. Now we are repeating this rent reduction issue, and it must be done. There are three points that we should first declare: 1. This rent reduction association is a genuine organization of awakened citizen tenants, an automatic new organization of action, and is not a continuation of the old organization last year. 2. The reason why we want to establish this rent reduction association is entirely based on the will of all citizens, and is based on the general requirements of the factual environment. 3. The meaning of issuing this propaganda publication is that all Shanghai citizens, whether they are real estate owners or tenants, must understand that the purpose of our request for uniform rent reduction this time is not only for the sake of tenants, but also for the benefit of real estate owners. In short, it is for the entire social class of happiness. Shanghai is the center of industry and commerce, and also a place where culture and talent gather. If we can follow the principle of co-existence and co-prosperity in a rational and proper way, and achieve the goal of reducing rents, so that citizens can live and work in peace and contentment, and Shanghai society can have the opportunity to prosper and revive, that is what this association hopes for."

Yunnan-Burma Boundary Survey Committee Scheduled to Depart from Nanjing 90

According to the Shin Shi News Agency, after the Chinese and British governments exchanged notes and agreed, the Chinese-British Yunnan-Burma Boundary Survey Committee has been established. The names and experiences of the three committee members are as follows: (1) The neutral committee member is Swiss Colonel Iselin, who served as the neutral chairman of the Syria-Iraq Boundary Survey Committee. (2) Chinese committee members: 1. Liang Yugao, Counselor of the Ministry of Railways, Advisor of the Treaty Committee of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs; 2. Yin Mingde, Advisor of the External Treaty Committee, who was previously sent by the External Ministry to Yunnan-Burma to investigate the recent situation of the boundary line. (3) British committee members: 1. Mr. Jewel Grose, Mr. F. S. Grose. In addition, both China and Britain have sent many experts and staff members. Our committee members and their entourage have decided to depart from Nanjing on September 10th. Before departing, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will convene a discussion meeting to instruct on the points that should be paid attention to. As for the route to Yunnan, there are two routes, one by water and land, taking a boat from Shanghai to Hong Kong, then taking the Yunnan-Vietnam Railway from Hanoi, Vietnam to Kunming; the other is to enter Yunnan via Sichuan. At that time, in order to save travel time, most people will take a boat from Nanjing to Chengdu, then charter a China Aviation aircraft from Chengdu to Kunming. As for the neutral and British committee members, they have already prepared to depart and are expected to gather completely by the beginning of December. The survey period is tentatively set for half a year and can be completed around May next year.

Dr. Pound Passed Through Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon to Return to the United States; Scheduled to Come to China Again Next Year to Lecture 91

Dr. Pound, the world-renowned jurist and Dean of the Law School of Harvard University, and his wife, after passing through Shanghai to Hong Kong, returned to Shanghai yesterday morning at 10:30 AM aboard the Chang Hing Company's "Empress of Russia" steamer. After disembarking at Gonghexiang Wharf on East Broadway Road, he was accompanied by Wu Jingxiong, chairman of the Faith and Constitution Committee, to visit Legislative Yuan President Sun Ke at 11:00 AM. After a long talk for one and a half hours, he bid farewell and went to the International Hotel on Jing'an Temple Road to attend a banquet hosted by the Harvard University Alumni Association. At 6:30 PM that evening, he took the original "Empress of Russia" steamer to return to the United States. Wu Jingxiong and many Harvard alumni went to see him off. Dr. Pound is scheduled to come to China again at the end of next year to lecture at the Soochow University Law School in Shanghai and other schools.

Secretary of the Siamese Ministry of Economy Secretly Arrived in Shanghai; Investigating the State of Sino-Siamese Trade; Trying to Alleviate the Anti-Siamese Rice Sentiment 92

According to the Shin Shi News Agency, since our country's people advocated boycotting Siamese rice and helping overseas Chinese in Siam in order to awaken the Siamese government, there has been panic in the internal affairs of Siam. The Siamese government has repeatedly discussed countermeasures. In addition to slightly accommodating compulsory education and immigration, literacy tests, etc., it has also sent Nai Wijuet, secretary of the Ministry of Economy, to China for investigation. Nai was formerly the secretary of the Ministry of Education and was the most active person in cracking down on overseas Chinese education. His mission this time is to conduct on-the-spot inspections of the state of Sino-Siamese trade and our country's anti-Siamese rice situation, hoping to find ways to alleviate the sentiment. Nai set off from Siam at the beginning of last month and first went to Hong Kong and Guangdong to investigate. According to news from overseas Chinese organizations in this port, Nai arrived in Shanghai from Hong Kong the day before yesterday, but his whereabouts are very secret. His attendant is Chinese lawyer Zeng Yaoyuan. Zeng grew up in Nanyang and studied in England. He is now a lawyer in Siam. He has lived in Siam for a long time and is extremely ignorant of the situation in his motherland. This time, he was invited by Nai Weile to come to China with him and plans to use Zeng's Chinese name to lobby the Chinese people on behalf of the Siamese government and promote propaganda for the Siamese government.

New Cotton Slightly on the Market; Excellent Quality, Prices Relatively Weak 93

According to the Hua Dong News Agency, in previous years, cotton samples were seen as early as before the half-month of the waste calendar in July. This year, due to the severe drought in early summer, the development of cotton buds was damaged, followed by continuous rain, resulting in late ripening of cotton in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. In addition, there was too much rain, which caused the cotton stalks to rise sharply, but the flowers were sparse, and the fruiting period was delayed. New cotton has only recently come on the market, more than ten days later than usual. Some of the arrivals include about 100 bales of Yuyao cotton. Hankou has also seen arrivals. According to observations by yarn factories, the quality of the new cotton is better than last year, but the price is quite weak, only about 31 to 32 yuan per unit.

Egg Exports Increased Sharply in July This Year; Ranked First Among Export Goods 94

According to the Shin Shi News Agency, since my country's eggs and egg products have declined in exports in recent years due to various influences, exports suddenly increased in July this year. According to customs statistics, in July this year, the national exports of dried egg white were 1,191,958 yuan, dried egg yolk was 612,732 yuan, dried eggs not divided into yellow and white were 206,215 yuan, frozen wet egg white was 246,848 yuan, frozen wet egg yolk was 441,796 yuan, frozen wet egg products not divided into yellow and white were 2,134,401 yuan, fresh eggs were 375,959 yuan, preserved eggs were 13,956 yuan, totaling 5,223,785 yuan, which increased compared to the same period last year and in June, ranking first among export goods in July. From January to July this year, the national exports of eggs and egg products still decreased compared to the same period last year. Among them, dried egg white exports were 5,521,451 yuan, dried egg yolk was 1,976,878 yuan, eggs not divided into yellow and white were 660,920 yuan, frozen wet egg white was 644,926 yuan, frozen wet egg yolk was 1,661,967 yuan, frozen wet eggs not divided into yellow and white were 6,846,580 yuan. Fresh eggs were 1,835,557 yuan, preserved eggs were 142,087 yuan, totaling 19,020,366 yuan, which decreased slightly compared to the export volume of 19,251,845 yuan in the same seven months last year.

City Chamber of Commerce Explains the Starting Standard for Stamp Tax: Reference to Tax Rate for Exempt Portions Should Be Made 95

Since the Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce held a stamp tax lecture and the "Commercial Monthly" published a special issue on the new stamp tax law, businesses in this city have gained a clearer understanding of the new law. Those with questions have made written inquiries, which the Chamber has answered in detail. Yesterday, the Chamber issued a notice to its members to explain in detail the starting amounts for stamp duty on contracts, subletting contracts, stock loans or mortgage contracts, inheritance or property division contracts, etc., stating: "Regarding the 'Brief Explanation of Stamp Tax Law' published in the Chamber's 'Commercial Monthly,' Volume 15, No. 8, Special Issue on Stamp Tax Law, in Section 1 of the 'Yin' category, there are phrases in the 'Tax Rate Table' such as 'Exempt if under ten yuan, or exempt if under fifty yuan.' The tax should only be calculated and stamped according to the 'count as one hundred yuan' example after the amount reaches fifty yuan or ten yuan. In Section 2, where there are no phrases in the Tax Rate Table stating 'exempt if under a certain amount,' the tax should be calculated and stamped according to the 'count as one hundred yuan' example, even if the amount is as small as one yuan or five yuan. The original intention is that although Clauses 15, 16, 17, 19, and 21 of the Tax Rate Table specify a tax of two cents for every hundred yuan, if the amount exceeds the exemption standard of less than ten yuan or less than fifty yuan, it should be taxed according to the example of every hundred yuan, even if it is less than one hundred yuan. Section 2 refers to Clauses 18 and 20 of the Tax Rate Table, which have no minimum exemption limit. Therefore, even if the capital raising for business and the bonds are as small as five yuan or one yuan each, they should be taxed at three cents per hundred yuan. That is the meaning of the word 'also.' However, the Tax Rate Table states, 'For amounts exceeding, but less than one hundred yuan, it should also be counted as one hundred yuan.' Therefore, the phrase 'also count as one hundred yuan' in the 'Brief Explanation,' which originally referred to the minimum limit, has been mistakenly understood to refer to the exceeding amount. There is a discrepancy in meaning here. Therefore, we are re-analyzing this specifically and will remove the word 'also' from 'also count as one hundred yuan' in Sections 1 and 2 of the 'Yin' category of the 'Brief Explanation of Stamp Tax Law' that has not yet been issued, to avoid misunderstanding."

Ning Shi Rehabilitation Preparation Office Established 96

Since the Ningbo Industrial Bank temporarily suspended its acceptance and settlement, the local Ningbo community and third parties have strongly advocated for its restoration, and the call for resumption has spread across the country. A restoration movement was organized within the Ningbo Tongxiang Association. Since its establishment, the Association has made smooth progress. Creditors have been actively signing up for shares, reaching 70% of the total debt. The initiators of the Association believe that the time for action is ripe. A fourth initiators' meeting was convened at the Central Western Restaurant on Fourth Malu a few days ago. It was resolved that the Ningbo Industrial Bank Rehabilitation Preparation Office would be established from today onwards. All initiators of the rehabilitation movement will continue to serve as preparatory committee members. In addition, five standing preparatory committee members will be elected to actively handle the resumption and capital increase. Once the creditor share subscriptions are completed, the resumption can be scheduled. The simplified rules for increasing shares for the resumption have been established, and the responsible persons of the office will be responsible for fundraising. The date of resumption should not be far off.

The Municipal Public Security Bureau Chief, Cai Jingjun, noted that Shanghai is a place where Chinese and foreigners live together, with a dense population. Beggars soliciting along the streets not only detracted from the city's appearance, but also hindered traffic. Therefore, he instructed the branch chiefs and police station chiefs to order their officers to pay attention at all times to the prohibition. He also contacted charitable organizations to send male and female beggars to beggar reception centers, training institutes, and vagrant work-study centers for resettlement. By 8:00 AM, more than fifty naked beggars were spotted. All were taken to the bureau for registration. At noon, these beggars were transported by vehicle to charitable organizations such as the Vagrant Work-Study Center for accommodation, in order to prevent them from wandering the streets and to improve the city's appearance.

Golden Pagoda Guessing Game Scholarship: Answers Revealed Yesterday: List of Winners to Be Announced at the End of the Month 102

The China Fuxin Tobacco Company believes that education is the foundation of the nation and industry is the source of national wealth. To make the country strong and prosperous, it is necessary to prioritize the popularization of education and the revitalization of industry. Therefore, in addition to making every effort to produce Golden Pagoda brand domestic cigarettes, the company has created the Golden Pagoda Scholarship to guide society and provide assistance to those who have lost their education. The method is to guess the time when Mr. Wang lost and found a pack of Golden Pagoda cigarettes. The answers are carefully sealed after verification and printing by Messrs. Shen Weiting, Zeng Xubai, Chen Yaozhu, Lu Shoulun, and Zhang Deqin, and stored in the Shanghai Bank. This is extremely fair and rigorous, and has been widely trusted by society.

The guessing game has been very popular. The game is simple. Even primary school students in the third and fourth grades can fill it out and participate. Therefore, there is an unprecedented number of participants. It is a rare and grand event.

Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM was the reveal of the answers. A special unveiling ceremony was held at the Shanghai Tobacco Industry Association. Representatives from all walks of life were invited to attend and the gentlemen who oversaw the sealing were invited to oversee. First, Mr. Ge Xiongfu, a representative of the company, took the answers from the vault of the Shanghai Bank and handed them to the overseeing gentlemen, who verified them without error and opened them publicly.

The time of loss was 3:48 AM on the 1st, and the time of finding was 1:22 AM on the 2nd.

Because there are many participants in this guessing game, it will take time to sort out the entries. The company is trying its best to organize them. It will likely be completed within a few days. Therefore, the results of the guessing game will be published in the Shen Bao, Xinwen Bao, and Ta Wan Pao newspapers at the end of this month.

Various Organizations and Film Industry Representatives Mourn Zheng Zhengqiu Yesterday: Yuan Ludeng Chaired and Reported the Meaning of the Memorial: Plans for Memorial Items and Launching a Public Funeral 104

Yesterday at 2:00 PM, various organizations and film industry representatives from various places held a memorial service for Mr. Zheng Zhengqiu at the Lake Society on Guizhou Road. Approximately 1,500 representatives from all walks of life and guests attended. Mayor Wu, Pan Gongzhan, and Yuan Ludeng chaired. The atmosphere at the venue was solemn. The details are as follows:

Venue Arrangement. A large black gauze banner with the white words "Memorial Service for Mr. Zheng Zhengqiu" hung over the entrance to the venue. There were also similar large horizontal banners in front of the entrance and the spirit seat. Banners were hung inside and outside the venue. A portrait of Mr. Zheng was hung in the center of the venue. An offering table was set up in front of the portrait, filled with incense, paper money, wine, and delicacies. Wreaths were arranged in front of the table, along with more than 20 stills from films directed by Zheng during his lifetime. Below was a square altar, the layout was simple, clean, and solemn.

Participants. In addition to all the male and female stars and staff of the Star Film Company and representatives of various sponsoring organizations, those who attended included Wang Xiaoji, Lin Kanghou, Yuan Ludeng, Wu Tiecheng (represented by Li Dachao), Zhu Xuefan, Pan Gongzhan, Yu Qiaqing, Shen Tianxin, Cai Chusheng, Sun Daosheng, Chen Dabei, Ren Jinping, Yan Duhe, Shi Dongshan, Jiang Yiping, Shao Xubai, Mao Yun, Guo Youcheng, Ma Dejian, and other guests from all walks of life, totaling approximately 1,500 people.

Agenda of the Memorial Service. 1. Opening, 2. Playing welcome music, 3. Ringing the bell, 4. Striking the drum, 5. Principal mourners take their positions, 6. Co-mourners take their positions, 7. Everyone stands at attention, 8. Principal mourners go to the portrait, 9. Playing mourning music, 10. Incense, 11. Offering flowers, 12. Reading the memorial text, 13. Singing the mourning song (by all actors of the Star Film Company), 14. Silence, 15. Bowing, 16. Family members express gratitude, 17. Playing mourning music, 18. Chairman returns to position, 19. Co-mourners return to position, 20. Giving the opening remarks, 21. Reporting on life and deeds, 22. Speeches, 23. Proposals, 24. Family members give a reply, 25. Playing farewell music, 26. Closing.

The Memorial Service. At 2:18 PM, the opening was announced. Chairman Wu Tiecheng (represented by Li Dachao), Pan Gongzhan, and Yuan Ludeng served as principal mourners, with Xu Yefu as master of ceremonies. After ringing the bell and striking the drum, the chairman's group offered incense and flowers. After Yan Gongshang finished reading the memorial text, all the male and female stars of the Star Film Company sang a mourning song. The sound was extremely sorrowful, and Hu Die and Gao Qianping even burst into tears. After the song, the bowing ceremony (three bows) was performed, and music was played before returning to their positions. Next, Yuan Ludeng, on behalf of the chairman's group, reported the meaning of the memorial, and Zhou Jianyun reported on his life and deeds. A proposal was made to purchase memorial items with donations from all parties and to hold a public funeral by various organizations in the future. Guests then gave speeches. Finally, Zheng Yingshi gave a thank-you speech on behalf of the family, after which music was played and the meeting adjourned.

Chairman's Report. Chairman Yuan Ludeng's report stated that today is the day when various organizations in this city mourn Mr. Zheng Zhengqiu. Everyone is aware of Mr. Zheng's life and the meaning of our memorial service, so I will not repeat it. We know that Mr. Zheng served society and worked hard to fulfill his responsibilities. His spirit of acting bravely for righteousness and not fearing fatigue, and the great undertakings he founded with his own hands, are truly admirable. Because he contributed to society and the nation, he should be mourned after his death. People living in the world, regardless of their age, should be judged by the value of the undertakings they founded during their lives. Mr. Zheng, in the short span of 30 years, abandoned his wealthy family and devoted himself to social undertakings, achieving today's success. His value is great, needless to say. I hope that those who participate in the memorial service today will follow Mr. Zheng's spirit and continue Mr. Zheng's undertakings, then the memorial will not be in vain. Zhou Jianyun then reported on Zheng's life and deeds, followed by Ren Jinping, Guo Youshou, Zhang Zhengfan, Jiang Jianbai, Chen Dabei, Cai Chusheng, Zhang Shichuan, and others who gave speeches, full of sorrow.

Memorial Text. On the 25th day of the 8th month of the 24th year of the Republic of China, the Guangdong Shanghai Fellow Association (omitting the names of thirty organizations) and others respectfully offer incense, flowers, and offerings to the spirit of Mr. Zheng Zhengqiu, saying: Oh, shining Mr. Zheng, the hero of the mountains of Lingnan, you were intelligent as a child and elegant as you grew up. With a clear style and firm ambition, you were both accommodating and wise, excelling in the arts and literature. You were not only skilled in managing affairs, but also treated people with sincerity. You were humble and self-disciplined, never presumptuous. You instructed us with kindness and beauty, and many were guided by your achievements. In the late Qing Dynasty, the country was in turmoil, with officials indulging in comfort and the people in ignorance. We followed the old ways until the country was destroyed. Mr. Zheng, you were alarmed by this and filled with sorrow. You thought hard and strived tirelessly, seeking guidance from history, especially from the writings of Mencius, using subtle satire and pointed admonitions to influence the ruler. You spent a lot of money on drama, not caring about giving up your wealth, and presented yourself as an example, gaining great fame and awakening the people. The great dream was awakened, and the spirit of the people rose. The revolutionary tide surged, and Mr. Zheng's achievements were relied upon by the world. You also valued education, especially popular education. You overcame the difficulties of producing films, presenting a true picture of society and opening the minds of the people. Western films were booming, while we were just starting. Mr. Zheng was saddened by this and worked tirelessly, forgetting the past and future. We were counting on his great talent and looking forward to his continued efforts. Who would have thought that his hard work would suddenly lead to his death? The masses have lost their guide, and the country has lost its talent. We think that even a hundredfold effort could not repay his contribution, and tears flow endlessly. This is not just personal grief, but the weeping of the entire society. Alas, please accept this offering!

Robbery of Rice Merchants in the Downtown Area: Thieves Suddenly Appear in the Athletic Field: Male and Female Thieves Arrested 105

At 1:50 AM yesterday morning, the Central District Branch received a report from the foremen of the athletic field, Liu Gupei, Yao Yongsheng, and Chen Zhiping, that at around 12:00 AM, more than ten robbers suddenly appeared in the athletic field. Several robbers wielded sharp knives and threatened them into silence, robbing six bags of rice stored in the field. After receiving the report, Branch Chief Huang Qiguang immediately ordered the chiefs and deputy chiefs of the Detective Squad, Wu Kezhong and Chu Jingwu, to lead detectives Lu Liuqing and Li Bingsen, along with patrol officers, to investigate. Zhang Desheng was arrested at No. 1 Jin Xujiazhai, and five measures of rice were seized. Five measures were seized at the home of Xue Mazi, but Xue Mazi had already escaped. Two pecks of rice and Western-style clothing were seized at the home of Jiang Fangshi at No. 4. The suspects and stolen goods were taken to the station. According to Zhang Guirong, an officer, Zhang Desheng confessed that he and a certain Hu Xingchang had obtained five pecks of rice and were preparing to divide it the next day. Jiang Fangshi confessed that her husband, Jiang Jiafa, had returned to his hometown in Anhui half a month ago. The rice was taken from the athletic field by her lover Min Guo, Chen Sanmazi, Jiang Jiafa, Zhou Rihe, Zhang Desheng, Hu Xingchang, Xue Mazi, and a certain Zhu. A suspect named Liu Huan claimed that he had gone out to urinate and was arrested. He said he did not know about the rice robbery. After verifying the confessions, the interrogating officer sent detectives Lu Liuqing and Li Bingsen to investigate. According to nearby residents, they knew that the thieves were behaving improperly, so they refused to rent them houses. Unexpectedly, Xu Boquan, the landlord of No. 4, rented a house to the thieves. The two detectives reported the situation. The Detective Squad found that Xue Yushan (aka Xue Mazi) was from Shandong. In July of last year, he had conspired to rob the San Mori Construction Factory on Hongqiao Road. The robbery was solved by Caojiadu Branch Detective Squad Chief (aka Wu Kezhong), and the robbers, including Li Weiyuan, were sent to court and sentenced to seven years in prison, while Xue Mazi was at large. Officer Zhang determined that Zhang Desheng had admitted to robbing rice with Hu Changxing, and Jiang Fangshi had testified that Zhang Desheng and Hu Changxing were involved, confirming the conspiracy to rob. As the main suspect, Xue Mazi, and others were at large, in addition to arresting the accomplices to investigate, the case was reported to the Public Security Bureau for disposition.

According to the Datong News Agency, after the Huafeng Xingji Flour Mill on Xiaoshadu Road was closed, the workers had not been dismissed. Absurd Report of Drowning, Seduction, Rape and Murder Failed, Wu Langqing Deceives Friend, Losing Morality, Cai Yongqing Returns from the Dead 107

Cai Fusheng, currently running the Sanyang Native Products Store in Qingdao, is 50 years old and a native of Ningbo. His wife, Zhu, is 52 years old. They have two sons, the elder named Zhenmiao and the younger named Yongqing, who is 29 years old and works as a cook on the Changxing steamship of the Sanbei Shipping Company. During the January 28th Shanghai Incident, Yongqing, through an introduction, married a woman surnamed Qi, named Xiaomao (28 years old this year), in Shanghai. After Qi married into the family, she lived with Yongqing at No. 4 Yong'an Lane, Chenxiangge Street, inside the Old North Gate of Shanghai City. In June of this year, Yongqing set off from Shanghai to Qingdao to borrow money from his father, Cai Fusheng, for use. At that time, Fusheng's wife, Zhu, because her son Yongqing had not returned home for a long time, and it was the height of summer with extremely hot weather, stayed at the store to avoid the summer heat before returning to Shanghai. At that time, Yongqing, unable to disobey his mother's wishes, agreed to stay in Qingdao. However, he had not notified his wife through a letter. Unexpectedly, Wu Langqing, a fellow villager of Cai, 25 years old, who originally had a good friendship with Yongqing and lived in the same place, but was not yet married, saw that Qi was quite attractive and had long plotted to have an illicit relationship, but had no opportunity. Wu, taking advantage of Yongqing's departure to Shanghai, lied to Qi, saying that Yongqing, due to the family's financial difficulties, deliberately went to Qingdao to borrow money as an excuse and had already taken a boat and committed suicide by drowning. The news was accurate, and so on. Qi suddenly heard Wu's words and thought to herself that her husband Yongqing had been away for a long time and there was no news, so she believed it to be true. She cried out in despair. After Wu persuaded her in many ways, she set up a spirit tablet at home to offer sacrifices and invited monks and Taoists to chant scriptures to save the soul of the deceased. Thereupon, Wu took the opportunity to seduce Qi, who was young and weak-willed, and she fell into his trap and became involved with him. When Yongqing's elder brother heard about it, he wrote a letter to Qingdao to inquire with his parents about the truth. Yongqing saw the letter and was greatly shocked. He quickly said goodbye to his parents and rushed back to Shanghai on the 22nd of the month. Just as he was about to return home, his neighbors, fearing that something unfavorable would happen to him, advised him not to return home to avoid danger. Yongqing had no choice but to return to the Changxing ship, intending to find a way to deal with it. Unexpectedly, Wu Langqing had already found out about it and used a preemptive strike. He secretly hid a sharp knife and boarded the Changxing ship on the previous evening at around 10 PM, intending to murder Yongqing. However, his plan was not well-kept and was heard by Yongqing's cousin, named Zhu Zhongxing, who quickly told Yongqing all the news and secretly discussed a method of arresting him. They agreed to wait together by the side of the 16th pier, No. 10 on the Bund in Nanshi. Before long, they saw Wu shuffling along. They managed to step forward and grab him, and called the watchman police officer Song Xigui from the 39th post of that place. They found a sharp small knife on Wu Langqing's body and took him to the 16th Sub-bureau. When the head of the Huang sub-bureau pre-tried the case, the plaintiff complained about the previous situation and requested a strict investigation. When questioned, the defendant Wu Langqing's confession was evasive. Because the case was important, he was ordered to prepare a document to be submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Fire Broke Out Again in Yangjia Ferry, Pudong, Still in the North Caonitang Area, Burning Down Fifteen or Sixteen Straw Sheds 108

In Yangjia Ferry, Pudong, on the west end of Heng Street, north of North Caonitang, there were many straw sheds. Yesterday, at 1:40 PM, a fire suddenly broke out in the shed where Guo Quanming from Hebei and Zhang Er from Tongzhou lived. They were unable to put it out, and the flames immediately broke through the roof of the shed and spread outwards. The head of the Yangjia Ferry Police Station, Yang Zhongquan, heard the alarm and quickly telegraphed to various fire departments for assistance. Meanwhile, in light of the severe fire in North Caonitang the previous time, he dispatched many more police officers to the fire scene to maintain order and assist. Soon, the director of the Pudong District Fire Brigade, Zhao Longsheng, led his staff to drive to the scene to provide assistance. After a while, fire trucks from Laobaidu and other places also arrived to help. However, at that time, the weather was hot and the straw sheds were extremely dry, so pouring a large amount of water had no effect. The fire burned more and more fiercely. Seeing that the situation was not good, the firefighters quickly joined forces to tear down the straw sheds around the fire and isolate them from the flames, which finally had a great effect. The fire could no longer spread, and its momentum weakened. The firefighters continued to do their best to extinguish the fire. At around 4 PM, the fire was completely extinguished. A total of fifteen or sixteen straw sheds were burned down and more than twenty were demolished. Afterwards, Director Yang ordered the two households where the fire started, Guo Quanming and Zhang Er, to be taken to the station for investigation into the cause of the fire. However, Guo pointed to Zhang, saying that the fire was started by frying beans, while Zhang pointed to Guo, saying that the fire was started by smoking opium. They passed the buck to each other. The director prepared a document and submitted it to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Yangjia Ferry Police Station Requests Construction of Civilian Housing to Accommodate Caonitang Fire Victims; General Bureau Submits to Municipal Government for Approval 109

A major fire broke out in North Caonitang, Yangjia Ferry, Pudong, at around 8 PM on July 29th of this year, burning down more than 700 straw sheds, with approximately 2,800 victims, men, women, and children. The details were previously reported. It is now learned that Yang Zhongquan, the head of the Yangjia Ferry Police Station, under whose jurisdiction the area falls, noted that in recent years, there have been four major fires in the north and south Caonitang areas. Most of the victims are coolies and workers from Jiangbei, a very large slum in this city. If strict measures are taken, these people will inevitably cause trouble unreasonably. If they are not prevented, they will rebuild on the same site after the disaster, without any fear. This situation is not a fundamental solution. Therefore, he recently suggested to the General Bureau that, referring to the plan to rebuild civilian housing on Qimei Road and other places in this city, he requested the Municipal Government to order the Civilian Welfare Committee to rebuild all the straw sheds in the north and south Caonitang areas into civilian housing. Although the land belongs to the Sand Industry Association, a method of renting land to build houses can be agreed upon with the association, and it can be used. It is heard that this proposal has been approved by the Bureau Affairs Meeting and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval. The local Party headquarters and various public organizations, believing that this move is related to civilian welfare, have also risen up to support it, striving to achieve the goal.

The Railway Bureau Offers Generous Compensation to the Stationmaster; Cai Lianqing's Coffin Was Received Yesterday 110

Cai Lianqing, the stationmaster of the Meilong Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, was run over and killed by the No. 1 express train from Beijing to Hangzhou at 2:50 PM the day before yesterday while on duty. Zhou Shifa Sued by Cousin for Seizing Ancestral Fortune Worth 600,000 Gold; Shifa Denies Ancestral Property 111

Zhou Shifa, a compradore for the De Fu Foreign Firm on Sichuan Road and a native of Shaoxing, is a cousin of Zhou Shizhen. Shifa is in his forties and is the elder brother, while Shizhen is only 25 years old and is the younger brother. In recent years, Shizhen has been living in Wuzhong, teaching at Minsheng Elementary School, earning only a little over ten yuan a month. His standard of living is worlds apart from that of his elder brother. When Shizhen's father passed away a few years ago, the family was very poor and could barely afford the funeral. Shizhen once begged his brother for help, appealing to their kinship, but Shifa only gave him fifty yuan. From then on, the cousins drifted apart and became like strangers. Recently, Shizhen, seeing that his brother possessed a huge fortune, all of which was inherited from their ancestors and belonged to the same lineage, believed that the inheritance should be divided equally. Therefore, he hired lawyer Mao Xianshen to file a lawsuit against Shifa in the First Special District Local Court to divide the property. He claimed that their ancestor Yunpu had four sons: Meng Peijun was the father of the defendant Shifa; Zhong Peidong had no children; Uncle Peizeng had one son, who disappeared early; and Ji Peilin was his father, who had two sons, one of whom also disappeared, and the other was him. His father and uncles had all passed away one after another. The ancestral property had never been divided, amounting to 600,000 yuan. It is now learned that the defendant has seized it all. He had previously requested the court to mediate, but the defendant refused, so he filed a lawsuit, requesting that the entire inheritance be handed over and divided according to law. Yesterday, Judge Ni opened the court and summoned both parties for interrogation. The plaintiff Zhou Shizhen testified that his father died in July of the 15th year of the Republic. His family also has two sisters: the elder, Xiujuan, is 22 years old, and the younger, Cangzhen, is only 18 years old. Before his father died, he told me that the ancestor had an inheritance of over 600,000 yuan, which had not been divided. Because the defendant's father was favored by his parents, he was in charge of managing the family property, and it was seized. When questioned, the defendant Zhou Shifa testified that when his father died, he was only eight years old. He was raised by his maternal uncle and then entered the De Fu Foreign Firm to work. His current property was earned by himself and there was no ancestral property. The court stated that further investigation was needed and ordered the hearing to be adjourned.

Muttering Incantations, Sealing Banknotes in a Can, 200 Yuan Vanished, Apprentice Realized He Had Been Fooled – Old Case from a Year Ago Finally Solved 112

Wang Weishan, a Zhenjiang native who uses playing cards to commit fraud, has been living on the sea, relying on it for many years. On June 12th of last year, Jin Fuyuan, an 18-year-old apprentice from Shangyu at the Kaishan Brick and Tile Company on Jiujiang Road, was ordered to go to the Wu Feng Qian Zhuang on Ningbo Road to collect 200 yuan in banknotes and bring them back to the company. When passing by Lane 498 on North Suzhou Road, Wang was there showing off his skills with two pages of playing cards, attracting onlookers. Jin stopped to watch, and they seemed to recognize each other. Wang, thinking that Jin was easy to deceive, said that he could not only teach this kind of magic trick, but also turn Jin's money into twice the amount. Jin was intrigued and asked for advice. Wang waited for the onlookers to disperse and then took out a tin can, ordering Jin to put all the 200 yuan banknotes into the can. He sealed the lid with red paper and smeared paste on the paper. While smearing, he muttered incantations, saying that he was drawing a talisman and reciting a spell. Then he handed the can to Jin to take home, firmly instructing him not to open it on the way. Jin returned to the company, thinking that he would unexpectedly get a windfall. He eagerly opened the lid and saw that the banknotes had turned into shredded newspaper, with a note attached, containing threats, roughly saying that heavenly secrets must not be revealed. If anyone asked him about the money, he should say that he encountered a thief on the way and was robbed of everything. The money would be returned after forty-nine days, otherwise he would be struck by lightning. At the end, it was written "Meet in the air." Jin then realized that he had been fooled and quickly told the company manager, who reported it to the police for investigation. After more than a year, they had no leads. Until recently, Jin happened to be walking at the intersection of Beijing Road and Zhejiang Road, and they unexpectedly met. He called the police and had him arrested by the Huishi Police Station. The day before yesterday, he was sent to the First Special District Local Court for interrogation. Wang Dashan confessed that he and an accomplice surnamed Ruan, who was still at large, had indeed defrauded Jin of money that day, and claimed that the banknotes in the can were replaced with newspaper when he shook the can up and down around the plaintiff. But the amount was only 162 yuan, and he got 47 yuan. The court ordered him to be detained and the hearing adjourned.

Appeal Filed by Robbers of Xinhua Bank; Overturning Testimony from First Instance 113

On the morning of June 4th of this year, at around 11 AM, three robbers broke into the Fourth Branch of the Shanghai Xinhua Savings Bank at the intersection of Xiafei Road and Hualong Road in the French Concession and robbed more than 4,700 yuan in cash. The robbers fled with the loot. When passing by Hehe Lane, they resisted arrest and shot and killed a pedestrian, a maidservant from Yangzhou named Wang Ma. They fled to the intersection of Chongqing Road in the Public Concession and shot and killed another male pedestrian. As a result, the robbers fled into Ma'an Lane and were caught on the rooftop of the kitchen at No. 28 in the lane. One of the robbers, a young man from Anhui named Wang Zhiting, was arrested, and a pistol was seized. He was taken back by the French police. It was found that the pistol belonged to Zhu Boyan (a native of Ningbo), a clerk at the Penghua Bank residing at No. 31 Continental Lane, Luban Road, which was already closed. Zhu was arrested along with Wang and sent to the Second Special Court. The case was prosecuted against Wang and Zhu for robbery, murder, and violation of the Regulations for the Suppression of Military Firearms. At the end of the trial, Wang Zhiting was sentenced to eight years in prison for robbery, but was found not guilty of murder. Zhu Boyan was fined 300 yuan for illegally possessing a pistol. The details have been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that the robber Wang Zhiting expressed dissatisfaction with the original trial verdict and filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court while in custody. The Higher Court, based on the petition, summoned witnesses the day before yesterday morning. President Liang Renjie, together with judges Sun Honglin and Wang Yue, specially opened the Third Court to interrogate them. The Police Department sent lawyer Yuan Jiahuang to court. The court first ordered the appellant Wang Zhiting to be brought to court and asked him about the reasons for his appeal against the original judgment. The defendant overturned the testimony from the original trial and tried to shift the blame to Zhang Zifa and others who were still at large, in an attempt to exonerate himself. The court then summoned witnesses and investigating detectives from the police station for questioning and ordered them to await a retrial on a set date. The appellant was returned to custody to await further instructions.

Chinese Institute of Engineers Awards Honorary Gold Medal to Hou Debang for His Diligent Efforts in Alkali Production 125

(Nanning Correspondence) The Chinese Institute of Engineers passed a resolution at its board meeting on June 24th of the 23rd year of the Republic of China that any citizen of our country who has made special contributions to engineering shall be awarded an honorary gold medal to commend their achievements. Recently, a proposal from ten members, including Gu Yuxiu, and the approval of the review committee, decided to award the first honorary gold medal at the annual meeting to Dr. Hou Debang, Chief Engineer of Yongli Chemical Industries in Tianjin. The awarding ceremony took place at 2:00 PM on the 13th of this month in the Guilin Grand Auditorium.

Hou, whose courtesy name is Zhiben, is from Minhou, Fujian. In the first year of the Republic of China, he graduated from Tsinghua School and was sent to the United States at the school's expense. He entered the Massachusetts Institute of Technology to specialize in chemical engineering, where he excelled. After obtaining his bachelor's degree in the sixth year of the Republic of China, he immediately interned in a chemical factory. Later, he entered Columbia University to continue his studies and obtained his master's degree in the eighth year of the Republic of China and his doctorate in philosophy in the tenth year of the Republic of China.

At that time, the Yongli Alkali Plant in Tanggu, Tianjin, was established, and Hou was hired as the chief engineer. Alkali is fundamental to the chemical industry, but foreign manufacturers kept the manufacturing methods absolutely secret, making it impossible to learn. After Hou was appointed in the United States, he immediately began designing, and after more than a year, he succeeded. In the eleventh year of the Republic of China, a Western mechanical engineer returned to China to install the machinery. After another year, the Yongli Alkali Plant began production. However, due to the vastness of the project and the constant difficulties, and with no specialized books for reference or experts to consult, all difficulties had to be solved by Hou himself. He devoted himself to research, and after more than a year, he achieved mass production, and Yongli became the earliest Solvay process alkali plant in East Asia. Currently, it produces 100 tons of soda ash per day, and it is expected to increase to 150 tons after autumn. In the nineteenth year of the Republic of China, Dr. Hou traveled to the United States for a second inspection. Recognizing the lack of reference books and materials on alkali production, he compiled his experiences into a special collection and published it to the world. It was published by the American Chemical Society as one of its series and was highly praised by experts from Western countries as a great work. In the twenty-first year of the Republic of China, he returned to China from the United States and added a caustic soda manufacturing department to the alkali plant. Later, he expanded the machinery factory and foundry. Now, all the newly added mechanical equipment in the Yongli Alkali Plant, whether large or small, precise or simple, can be manufactured in-house, making it a model for domestic factories. After the Yongli alkali production business had established a solid foundation, Hou devoted his remaining efforts to new ventures. At the beginning of the twenty-third year, Yongli Alkali Company was reorganized into Yongli Chemical Industries, adding an ammonium sulfate manufacturing department. The plant site is located in Puzhen, with a capital of seven million yuan. All engineering aspects are under Hou's direction. He traveled to the United States again in the spring to negotiate all equipment procurement matters and supervise the manufacturing of various equipment. Currently, all the machinery has been shipped to China in succession, and Dr. Hou will also return to China this autumn. It is expected that the ammonium sulfate plant will begin shipping goods next autumn.

Since Hou began serving at Yongli Company for alkali production, he has experienced countless difficulties and hardships over the past fifteen years. However, Hou, relying on his knowledge and experience, worked diligently and persevered until he succeeded. His perseverance and spirit are truly admirable. Moreover, Hou excels in both academics and business, not only laying the foundation for chemical engineering in our country but also having his specialized writings admired both at home and abroad, making him a glory of our country's engineering and academic circles. Now, the Chinese Institute of Engineers is awarding him an honorary gold medal, not only to express its admiration for Hou but also to hope that more Chinese people will follow Hou's example and strive for engineering academics and engineering construction.

Zhejiang Province's Children's Year to Open on September 7th 127

The preparatory committee for the opening ceremony of the Children's Year in Hangzhou, Zhejiang Province, held its first meeting at the Educational Hall at 3:00 PM on the 22nd. Present were 28 representatives from the standing committee of the Provincial and Municipal Children's Year Implementation Committee, various departments of the Provincial Government, the Provincial and Municipal Party Headquarters, and provincial and municipal educational and charitable organizations. Luo Di, Standing Committee Member of the Provincial Children's Year Implementation Committee, presided over the meeting. After the chairman reported on the progress of the work, the discussion began on the preparatory committee's charter, budget, and other matters to be carried out. The meeting adjourned at around 5:00 PM. The resolutions are recorded below:

1. Amended and approved the charter of the Zhejiang Provincial Children's Year Opening Ceremony Preparatory Committee. 2. Resolved to set the date of the Children's Year opening ceremony on September 7th (Saturday) at 8:00 AM at the West Lake Public Sports Field. 3. Amended and approved the budget for the Children's Year opening ceremony expenses. 4. Resolved to appoint the personnel in charge of this committee: (1) Three standing committee members, to be represented by representatives of the Provincial Children's Year Implementation Committee, the Municipal Children's Year Implementation Committee, and the Provincial Party Headquarters. (2) Directors of each group: General Affairs - Provincial Department of Education, Layout - Provincial People's Education Center, Recreation - Municipal Government, Publicity - Municipal Party Headquarters. (3) Staff of each group: General Affairs Group - Secretariat of the Provincial Government, Department of Civil Affairs, Department of Finance, Security Department, Provincial Relief Institute, Bureau of Commerce, Layout - Paper, Provincial and Municipal Sports Fields, Provincial Poor Children's Home, Provincial Women's Association, Hangzhou Children's Welfare Promotion Association, Central Air Defense School, Zhejiang Military Training Committee, Hangzhou Medical Association, Recreation Group - Provincial Public Security Bureau, National Arts Center, Municipal First, Second, Third, Fourth, and Fifth People's Education Centers, Municipal Boy Scout Council, Publicity Group - Department of Construction, Provincial Telephone Bureau, Zhejiang University, Central Aviation School, Provincial Library, Municipal Children's Library, Municipal Women's Association, Journalists Association. (4) The work of each group will be drafted by the directors of each group, who will convene a meeting of all staff within three days (the 24th, 25th, and 26th).

Recent News from the Labor Education Experimental Zone 128

The Ministries of Industry and Education, in order to actively promote labor education, jointly established the Labor Education Design Committee, and it was resolved to first establish labor education experimental zones in Shanghai, Wuxi, Tianjin, Qingdao, and Hankou. Last year, as the first step, the two ministries sent personnel to Shanghai and Wuxi to jointly establish labor education experimental zones in Shanghai and Wuxi with relevant agencies and organizations in the two locations. Currently, labor education in Shanghai and Wuxi is being promoted by the committee members (Pan Gongzhan in Shanghai and Gao Jian'si in Wuxi), and progress has been greater than last year. It is reported that the second step in the two ministries' plan for this year was originally to continue establishing labor education experimental zones in Tianjin, Qingdao, and Hankou. However, due to the floods in Hankou, it is necessary to suspend the plan, and only Tianjin and Qingdao can be established. Currently, the Ministries of Industry and Education are jointly drafting letters to the administrative authorities of Tianjin and Qingdao to first investigate the actual situation in each location, and after receiving a response, they will plan to establish the two labor education experimental zones.

Ministry of Education Establishes Editorial Committee for Educational Yearbook 129

(Nanjing, 25th dispatch) The Ministry of Education has established an editorial committee for compiling and printing the Chinese Educational Yearbook, appointing fifteen people, including directors of various departments, counselors, and senior secretaries and supervisors, as members of the editorial committee, and thirty people, including section chiefs and recommended secretaries and supervisors, as compilers.

New President of Sichuan University to Fly to Chengdu, Advocates No Changes to Faculty and Staff 130

(Special Dispatch from Beiping) Ren Hongjun, the newly appointed president of National Sichuan University, was originally the Executive Director of the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture. He studied in the United States in his early years and has long served in academic circles in Beiping after returning to China. After the government appointed Ren as president of Sichuan University, he went to Nanjing once for negotiations. Ren has now requested leave from the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture, and the foundation has approved a one-year leave. Ren will travel south today (the 24th), first to Nanjing to meet with Wang Shijie, the Minister of Education, for negotiations, and then fly to Hankou on the 27th and from Hankou to Chengdu on the 28th to prepare for his new position as president of Sichuan University. His wife, Ms. Chen Hengzhe, will stay in Beiping to teach. There are rumors in Beiping that Hu Shi will take the position of Dean of the Faculty of Arts at Sichuan University, but the position of Dean of the Faculty of Arts has already been appointed to Yang Zonghan, the head of the Department of Foreign Languages at Beiping Normal University. Regarding the faculty and staff of Sichuan University, Ren advocates that there should be no changes in principle.

Municipal Bureau of Education Orders All Schools to Participate in Confucius's Birthday Celebration, Tomorrow is a Holiday, and Flags Should Be Displayed to Mark the Occasion 131

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued an order to all large, medium, and small schools in the city, stating that it had received order number 15283 from the Municipal Government on the 23rd of this month, stating that the 27th of this month is the nationally designated memorial day for Confucius's birthday, and that there will be a holiday for one day. All sectors should display flags to mark the occasion. A memorial meeting will be convened at 10:00 AM on that day, gathering representatives from all sectors at the Dacheng Hall of the Municipal People's Education Center on Wenmiao Road in the Nanshi district. In addition to sending separate notices and announcements, the bureau is hereby ordered to promptly comply and instruct its subordinate staff to attend the meeting on time and participate. It is also ordered to instruct subordinate educational institutions in the city to send representatives to participate in the memorial meeting. This order is issued by the Director of the Bureau, Pan Gongzhan.

This City's June Education Fees Will Be Issued the Day After Tomorrow, and Subsidies for Private Schools Will Be Issued at the Same Time 132

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued a notice stating that the bureau will issue the regular expenses for municipal schools and social education institutions for June and the subsidies for private schools for June on August 28th (Wednesday) from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM and from 1:00 PM to 3:30 PM. Each municipal school and institution should submit the calculation basis for all expenditures prior to June to the bureau before the payment and come to the bureau on time to collect the funds. Furthermore, as the current academic year has begun, starting from August, each municipal school and institution should resubmit their seals for verification. Blank seal paper can be requested when collecting fees. This notice is hereby issued for your information.

Shou Yicheng's Farewell to the Working Youth of Hangzhou 133

Dr. Shou Yicheng, an economics expert, served in an important banking position in Hangzhou for four years and achieved considerable success. He offered many suggestions to the working youth of Hangzhou. Yesterday, he published an article entitled "Farewell to the Working Youth of Hangzhou," which included eight key points: (1) Maintain vitality with an optimistic attitude; (2) Overcome the environment with a strong will; (3) Create career opportunities with a professional spirit; (4) Develop a healthy character with a straightforward demeanor; (5) Cultivate economic independence by advocating thrift; (6) Expand knowledge through continuous research; (7) Unleash inner potential by making good use of strengths; (8) Realize career plans with thorough preparation. He also said that the motivation of any promising young person engaged in any industry must be extremely pure, their direction must be extremely lofty, and their actions and steps must be extremely firm and practical. The above-mentioned points are all cultivation efforts that we must go through to seek this, and the key to success lies precisely in this. Experts in factory management have said that apprentices are the most important basic component in an industrial organization, and the success or failure of a business can be seen in the success or failure of apprentice training. Therefore, our young comrades, no matter what industry they are engaged in or what position they hold, should have the conviction of not belittling themselves and doing their best. If I am absent, not only will a basic member be lost in this business, but also an important driving force will be lost in the national movement to revitalize the Chinese nation and promote economic construction. Therefore, each should work diligently and strive for progress in their respective positions, and I need not worry that they will have no way to serve. I am incompetent, but I have always encouraged myself to be a youth-oriented employee, and I often express my heartfelt feelings in the hope of encouraging each other. I hope to inspire others by offering my humble opinions, especially at this moment of reluctant farewell.

Telegram from the National Language Association, Suzhou Phonetic Symbols to Be Tested Regularly, Closing Ceremony Scheduled for Tomorrow Afternoon at 1:00 PM, 301 Suzhou Phonetic Little Teachers Have Been Recruited 135

The Fang Jin Committee of the National Association for the Promotion of Mandarin Education, in order to promote Suzhou phonetic symbols, has been broadcasting lessons on the Shanghai Buddhist Music Radio Station every day from 2:15 PM to 3:00 PM since August 1st of this year. It is reported that the course has been completed and a test will be given in mid-September to award prizes. The following is a summary of various news items:

301 Suzhou Phonetic Teachers. The association began recruiting Suzhou Phonetic Teachers on August 1st and recruited a total of 301. Boys accounted for 58% and girls accounted for 42%. The ages of the young teachers were: 7% were 10 years old, 8% were 11 years old, 10% were 12 years old, 21% were 13 years old, 29% were 14 years old, 14% were 15 years old, and 6% were 16 years old. The levels of the young teachers were: 31% were in junior high school, 43% were in senior primary school, 15% were in junior primary school, and 10% were unknown.

More than 1,000 students have been taught. The Suzhou Phonetic Teachers either listened to the lessons at home or at the Suzhou Park Library. After learning, except for 74 people, all of them taught students according to the rules. 59 people taught one person, 72 people taught two people, 13 people taught three people, 11 people taught four people, 5 people taught five people, 4 people taught six people, 12 people taught seven people, 11 people taught eight people, 3 people taught nine people, 1 person taught ten people, 6 people taught eleven people, 5 people taught twelve people, 3 people each taught thirteen and fourteen people, 4 people taught fifteen people, 2 people each taught sixteen and eighteen people, 1 person taught seventeen people, and 1 person each taught nineteen to twenty-eight people, totaling 1,132 people. The oldest was 13 years old and the youngest was 7 years old. Boys accounted for 73% and girls accounted for 27%.

The closing ceremony and regular test. The association will hold the closing ceremony of the radio broadcast on August 27th at 2:15 PM at the Shanghai Buddhist Music Radio Station: (1) Music, (2) Closing remarks, (3) Report, (4) Singing (Flood Song), (5) Opera fan stories (Green Building Dream), (6) Little Hothead (Harmony Brings Prosperity), (7) Singing (Don't Commit Suicide), (8) Closing remarks. The association, in order to test the listening results, will give a copy of the Suzhou Mandarin Vocabulary to those who correctly answer nine questions and the first series of 30 books of the Suzhou Phonetic Series to those who correctly annotate ten phonetic symbols. It is also reported that the test date has been set for September 8th and 15th, to be held simultaneously in Shanghai and Suzhou. Young teachers with excellent results will receive school funding and prizes to help them maintain their interest.

News from Various Schools 138

Pei Zhen Primary School

Pei Zhen Primary School and Kindergarten at 875 Haig Road in this city was founded in the ninth year of the Republic of China by Shen Shukui, a former leader in the education field. In the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, Madam Ling Hongxun (the late Ms. Ling Shilan) added a kindergarten. In the eighteenth year of the Republic of China, it was moved to its current location due to expansion. The school's teaching is effective, and management is strict. It opened on the 22nd of this month. It is currently reported that there are some vacancies in each grade, and whether students are day students or boarders, arrangements can be made.

Ci Hang Advanced Midwifery School

Wang Xuequan, the principal of Ci Hang Advanced Midwifery School at the intersection of Hedde Road and Changping Road in this city, is very interested in running midwifery education. Students from far and near admire the school's reputation, and there are countless people who have requested to enter the school. It is now known that the school is scheduled to open on the 26th of this month, and classes will begin on the 2nd of September. It is also reported that in order to avoid disappointing students from afar, Principal Wang has specifically set September 5th as the last entrance examination for this semester.

Min Li Middle School

Min Li Middle School at the Great South Gate, in view of the lack of educational opportunities for general working youth, has specifically submitted an application to the Bureau of Education to add a commercial night class. The level is divided into senior and junior levels, as well as various elective courses. The class time is from 7:00 PM to 10:00 PM every day. The term is three years for both junior and senior levels. In the future, the qualifications after graduation will be equivalent to those of middle school.

Hu Nan Primary School

Hu Nan First Primary School on Huangjiaque Road in the West Gate held its commencement ceremony yesterday. More than 300 teachers and students attended. Principal Mao Zhilan reported on the development plan for this semester and added three teachers, all graduates of the Municipal Wuben Women's Middle School. In order to encourage students' studies, the school has established free places. Those who have excellent character and academics and an average score of A or above will be eligible for free tuition. There are currently vacancies in each grade.

Min Guang Middle School

Since Tang Zenghui and Xu Zexiang have been responsible for Min Guang Middle School at No. 2 Jiaozhou Road, the number of students has been increasing day by day. There are more than 500 new and old students this semester, and the girls' dormitory has been expanded to accommodate them. Therefore, there is considerable guidance and support for the graduation students' further education and employment problems. The school's directors, such as Zhang Daofan, are currently members of the National Government and Deputy Minister of Transportation. Liu Hongsheng is currently the General Manager of the China Merchants Group. Wu Xingya is the current Director of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs. There are also banking giants Wang Yansong and Xi Yushu, Legislative Yuan member Wu Kaixian, Military Commission Counselor Ding Mocun, Shanghai Local Association President Du Yuesheng, and Tang Baoshu, Zhu Yingpeng, Tong Hangbai, and Dong Renjian as school directors. Therefore, half of the graduating students in the general business and vocational business courses this semester have been admitted to national and famous private universities, and more than half have already been employed. It is also reported that the school provides free admission to students who have excellent conduct and academic performance. It is now known that the students who performed well last semester and are eligible for free tuition this semester are Huang Rongji and Xiong Nuchao in the Senior General Department, Yu Xianglin in the Senior General Department One, Wang Deyuan in the Senior Business Department Two, Zhuang Shuguang, Shi Jianwu, and Sun Wenqin in the Junior Middle School Three, and Liu Housheng, Shen Qiang, and Yuan Shaomo in the Junior Middle School One.

Little Boy (20) (6) 139

— Original by Ms. Alcott of America, translated by Zheng Xiaocang (Zonghai)

Once, when his grandmother was invited to dinner, he put cobblestones in the sugar bowl - the poor old lady wondered why they wouldn't dissolve in her tea, but she was so well-mannered that she didn't say anything. Once in church he passed a snuff bottle all the way down the aisle, so five boys sneezed so badly they had to leave in a hurry. In winter he dug a little path in the snow, then secretly poured cold water on it, and soon people were falling all over the place. He almost drove poor Mr. Rice crazy because he hung Mr. Rice's big boots in a conspicuous place, and Mr. Rice's feet were enormous, which was exactly what he didn't want people to know. He advised the good little Daoli to tie a thread to his loose tooth and let one end of the thread dangle outside his mouth when he fell asleep so that Tao Mo could pull it out for him without feeling the pain of the operation. However, the tooth didn't fall out when it was pulled the first time, and poor Daoli woke up in pain and never trusted Tao Mo from that day on. The last prank was to deliberately soak bread in wine and feed it to the hens, making them dizzy and staggering, while other poultry ran away at the sight, because those usually dignified old hens were suddenly stumbling and staggering, pecking and crowing. The whole family laughed so hard at these strange appearances until little Mei pitied them and locked them in the chicken coop to sleep off their drunkenness.

These were the boys here, and they lived together very happily, studying, playing, working, arguing, overcoming mistakes, and cultivating virtues together. The children of other schools may have more book knowledge, but when it comes to the understanding or insight that makes people good, I'm afraid they are not as good as here. Words and mathematics are certainly very good, but in Professor Pei Er's opinion, self-awareness, self-help, and self-control are even more important, and he did teach them these things very carefully. Others sometimes shook their heads when talking about his ideas, even though they admitted that the children had made extraordinary progress in their behavior and manners. But we should naturally know, as Mrs. Shu said to Ned, this is a "strange school."
