Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

Crowning of the Standard Beauty 179

— Lang

This year, the extent of the flooding in our country, the breadth of the affected area, and the severity of the loss of life and property for the people are almost impossible to calculate. Therefore, this flood is not only more severe than the people remember, but it is also the most unprecedented catastrophe in recent decades. However, our country's society is subjected to the dumping of foreign goods from the outside, and the bankruptcy of rural areas from the inside. The market is sluggish, industry is in decline, and the economy is depleted. The ability to provide disaster relief is almost zero. Therefore, we have to use the term "entertainment without forgetting disaster relief" to call for support, which is originally a "laughing through tears" kind of thing.

Logically speaking, the seriousness of such a flood and the tragic cries of the famine victims should naturally prompt all our compatriots who have not suffered this disaster to act with conscience and donate generously for emergency relief. Originally, there was no need to make a big fanfare under the names of various art performances and beauty pageants to call for support. If disaster relief efforts have to resort to such titles to appeal to the public, then the general audience will only think of entertainment and not of the disaster victims. Judging from such charitable efforts, it is not only possible to infer the weakness of the sense of compassion among the Chinese people, but it is also a complete demise of human morality.

Using art performances to help disaster relief is originally an unfortunate act of "healing the immediate wound at the cost of cutting out the heart". It also takes advantage of the psychological weaknesses of our compatriots to accomplish this. Therefore, whether Xu Lai deserves the title of "Oriental Standard Beauty" or not is not worth discussing. Even if she does, the election is over and it's done. There is no need for so-called crowning and awarding titles, or to further embellish the event and promote each other. It is not only ridiculous to the world, but it also insults the personality of contemporary ladies. It is appropriate that the Chinese Women's Progressive Association has voiced its strong disapproval.

Promoting extravagance and encouraging frivolity are originally vices of society. Moreover, at a time when the New Life Movement is being promoted and the social economy is declining, such actions are contrary to the current trends of life. Even in terms of disaster relief efforts, if the association spends one less penny, the disaster victims will receive one more penny of relief. If the association spends one more penny, the famine victims will receive one less penny of aid. Assuming that without such absurd and ridiculous actions, it would not be enough to attract a large audience, it should be known that the cost of various expenses incurred by this event is also considerable. I am afraid that the gains do not outweigh the losses.

Therefore, if we speak profoundly about this kind of ridiculous behavior, it is a mentality of gloating over misfortune. In terms of facts, it is also taking advantage of the opportunity to gain personal vanity. In short, the purpose of this disaster relief art performance was originally to help the disaster victims. If the purpose can indeed be achieved, benefiting both the public and private sectors, it is originally a passive relief measure. If it is only in name and not in reality, nominally for disaster relief, but the famine victims receive little benefit, only adding to this meaningless action, then one cannot help but sigh deeply.

Random Notes in Early Autumn 180

— Family Member

1. A Wanderer's Emotions

Standing alone in the autumn wind, September's clothes remain uncut.

In the evening, with nothing to do, I stood by the window, quietly gazing at the sky gradually enveloped in twilight. When a gust of evening wind with a hint of coolness blew against my face, I couldn't help but silently recite two lines of poetry by the ill-fated poet Huang Zhongze, which I could never forget. As a result, my mood immediately sank into a state of melancholy. My seemingly frozen emotions rippled slightly. My thoughts began a lonely, sorrowful journey. No one believes that time flies by so quickly. Remembering the autumn when I left home, it seems as clear as if it were just yesterday, but counting it, it has already been the fourth autumn since then. During this time, I have crossed some oceans, and also crossed some cities and towns, as well as some villages. The long days of several years have all been very rushed, never staying in any place for a longer period of time, just like a very hardworking person, what is it ultimately for? Perhaps it is really for something, otherwise why would I push my body and mind so tirelessly? However, I do not know. I only know that I have indeed walked many roads and seen many things, but I have not obtained anything real. I have only earned boundless emptiness and a boundless feeling of vagueness. As for the result of long journeys, it has made me an extremely weary and meaningless tired person. And I have become a wandering soul with no hope, no joy, and even no emotions.

The coarse web of vulgar life will turn your emotions into lead weights. I think people are always pitiable, always passing from one season to another in such a muddleheaded way, year after year, and each season always pays me a heavy spiritual burden, and real worries and pressures. Wanderers never have a day of stability: the scorching summer seems easy to get through; once summer goes and autumn comes, the snowy winter days follow closely behind, and the winter clothes are locked inside the shikumen, and it is difficult to cope with ordinary days, so what leisure do I have to take them out? Thinking about it makes me shiver. But now I have no such worries at all, when the problems that cannot be solved exceed the power of a weak and sensitive emotion.

2. Deep Drunkenness at Midnight

With the heart of a young man, but filled with grey thoughts that a young man should not have, and perhaps even mixed with the languid breath of an old man. So I have the appearance of premature aging. In front of people, I also have the same laughter and interest in seeking entertainment as ordinary people. But these are not things that I am willing to do. Everything in the world is estranged and lonely to me. This estrangement and loneliness are also what I am used to. I have many words hidden in my heart, but there is no one I can reveal them to, and no one who is qualified to be worth telling them to, so I like to think and meditate on the distant. Every night, I stagger out of the hotel drunk, walking on the cold and lonely sidewalk. Only half a person is seen every half day, which does not hinder my unbridled behavior. I open my throat and sing and whistle, and if there is a moon in the sky, the moon is my only companion. Then I walk slowly on the moonlight, and the song becomes more energetic. If I'm not tired, it doesn't matter if I walk until dawn, because my grievances have disappeared invisibly. When I'm so sad that I can't get rid of it, I have to sink into such a state, although after waking up, there will inevitably be a more unbearable bitterness, I understand, but the temporary intoxication is finally a pleasure. At that time, it is almost half dreaming: my body is immersed in the moonlit color like a melted silver liquid, and the stars are shining on my head. My mood is excited, as if there is nothing in the world that makes people depressed, and I forget everything, although occasionally a few fallen leaves are blown down by the wind and swim past my front, reporting a little autumn news to me, but I have no time to pay attention.

Cooperation 181

Fruit 182

— Rong

There is a small round table in my room, with a plate on it, filled with fresh fruit—the sweet vegetables, the lovely fruit, the fruit that evokes longing.

When I am quiet, I often gaze at this agate-colored fruit plate in contemplation. This vegetable plate is a relic of our old family. It has witnessed the changes in this family—joy and sorrow, viewing and resentment, prosperity and decline—but it has always remained silent. Whenever fruit is on the market, different fruits will be pressed on its body by different hands. Now it is placed in this corner of the room, and whenever there is fruit, it will spread out a rich fragrance like flowers and trees. People who smell this fragrance will also feel as if they are in a fruit orchard with fragrant grass, beautiful flowers, and falling petals. The eternally fixed blue sky presents the peace of the universe, and the rich fruits match the joy of the people, making people unable to resist being fascinated by this realm. In imagination, there can be trees, ponds, and vegetable fruits swaying in the light red evening glow, or rolling on the green lawn, like yellow autumn leaves. Homeless birds come to peck at the half-green vegetable skins. When they carry them to mid-air, they fall down, sinking into the pond and disturbing the swimming fish coming and going... But when I open my eyes, it is still this small room, a pile of fruit quietly lying there, as if secretly laughing at your infatuation. In the dim twilight, a tone seems to come through: "Why don't you come and eat us? Shall we have a kiss?" The voice is like that of a beautiful young woman, and you can't help but turn your head back. When you turn your head back, there is nothing there. It is still the pile of fruit lying there motionless. The aged fruit plate is being pressed so hard that it can't breathe, stiff like an old woman carrying a heavy load.

There are yellow bananas, deep yellow and light red Florida oranges, purple or white half-ripe grapes, apples as plump as a seventeen-year-old girl, and peaches like fragrant courtesans. These are all mixed up, you pushing me and I squeezing you, lying in the plate. This kind of fresh, vibrant atmosphere forms a clear contrast with the ancient, powerless fruit plate. This pile sometimes looks even better than bottled flowers. In the soft light of the morning sun and in the green dim light of the night, there is such a poetic and hazy mood. I sometimes even want to pick up a pen and write a poem.

In order to satisfy my own appreciation, I can't bear to eat them. I feel that eating these lovely vegetables into my stomach, destroying the current decoration to satisfy my own appetite, is completely a discordant thing. Sometimes my hand has already stretched out, but I quietly withdraw it in a second thought. Once, all the fruit in the plate was rotten. With a feeling of cherishing, I threw them away and replaced them with a plate of exquisite crabapple fruit. They are all red, the sisters of cherries, the sisters of apples and vegetables, slender and withered green leaves, just like warm hair, diligently protecting the shy face. Once, my index finger moved, cruelly gnawing at her rosy cheeks and swallowing the sweet nectar of life into my stomach. The taste is very sour, a taste of love, a taste of wine, and with a touch of nostalgic sadness.

Now the crabapples in the plate are almost eaten up by me. I hope to go to the market tomorrow and buy some more lovely fruits. I can't let the plate be empty. Thinking of this, such brilliant colors appear in front of me again, and gentle or splashing colors fill my surroundings. I really hope that I can leave the market that I have to go to every day and run to the suburban vegetable and fruit orchard, sit under a big tree to read a book or smoke a cigarette, listen to the fish jumping in the pond, and easily pluck off a slightly green fruit, eating it while running over the hill to see the porcelain-like fields, and watch the big, red, tangerine-shaped sun at dusk...

Page 21

Zhaoshang Inn 183

— Hu Weixiong

Like the inns in ordinary small towns, they used "Zhaoshang Inn" as their signboard. But after so many merchants were attracted, the bald-headed innkeeper and the insomniac-like waiter were a little overwhelmed.

The dozen or so wooden tables were all full, and the ground was covered with water brought in. The waiter was already a bit clumsy, and this made it even more awkward for him to walk. He first handed out a wooden basin and several towels to each table, and then asked the customers one by one what dishes they wanted to eat. At this time, the innkeeper came to greet them. He was already covered in sweat, as if he had just crawled out of the stove. Some of the customers who had stayed overnight in Liuniao Bay asked the innkeeper to bring out some good wine first. So the innkeeper opened his broken bamboo throat: "There are only about a dozen jars of aged Huadiao wine in the inner room, and there are dozens of piles of top-quality white rice, but..." The innkeeper narrowed his eyes, looked up at the sky and laughed, showing his full-fledged philistine air. Then he gave a wink at the noisy crowd and said, "I'm really sorry, there's no place to buy fresh side dishes. Gentlemen, please help me with this, just so-so."

He laughed again, naturally drawing laughter from our group.

During the meal, people who didn't know each other became familiar. After everyone filled their stomachs, they thought of the clothes that had been soaked by the rain. The Zhaoshang Inn was quite like the northern style. With a shout from everyone, the insomniac-like waiter had already prepared charcoal basins for us under the direction of the bald-headed innkeeper. At this time, everyone's flushed faces were overflowing with a slight tipsiness. They all stripped off their wet clothes, as if they were on a snowy winter night, sitting around the fire basin, opening their clothes, and watching the water vapor being evaporated by the flames rise. For a moment, everyone sank into sweet memories, letting time pass quickly.

The heavy rain outside was still hitting the roof like thunder. I knew that everyone could clearly hear it: but under this almost Arabian Nights situation, no one wanted to think of the pain or loss caused by being blocked by the rain, which would cause this group to be unhappy, and even break the pleasure that everyone was quietly enjoying. The innkeeper and the waiter didn't know when they had hidden in the kitchen. When that steaming bald head reappeared before our eyes, his philistine laughter was like a sharp arrow, resonating in the wide dining hall.

"Gentlemen, would you like some strong tea?" As he said this, he stepped aside, and behind his huge pig-like body, the waiter was already holding a large tray with both hands, with a dozen cups of almost black strong tea steaming like the bald head. "It's raining heavily outside. I'm afraid the boat won't be able to sail tomorrow!" Then, of course, there was another series of laughter that made people frown.

After he said this, the huge sound of rain seemed to be sent into everyone's ears more clearly, but did you want to get angry at the innkeeper? He was like a cunning fox, stretching and shrinking his head, and so diligently delivering cups of tea to each guest. A businessman would never forget his business philosophy no matter what.

The water vapor on the clothes gradually thinned out. While we were silently drinking tea, exhaustion slowly climbed into everyone's heart. The innkeeper was as astute as ever. He was holding the candle and waiting for our instructions.

News Piece on Begging for Relief 184

Year after year, disasters do not cease, the disaster victims everywhere are heartbroken, natural disasters and man-made disasters, water and fire are raging, so the Yangtze River and the Yellow River are full of disaster victims, they are. The starving are waiting to be fed, with no food to eat, one by one. Drifting and starving to death, their lives returning to the underworld, desperately trying to survive, fantasizing about keeping their lives, begging for food from door to door, pitiful sounds constantly appearing on the streets, some are. Travelers fleeing through the rivers and lakes, some are. Vagrants living in the city, some are. Wives and children separated, wailing and crying, some are. No houses, no places to settle down, some are, sobbing and weeping, telling about the disaster situation, some are. Crying for help, some are, even more. Calling for brothers, looking for double observatories, seeking husband and wife; looking for children and grandchildren, abandoning their families, leaving their lovers, and even more. The tragic deaths of people drowning on the spot, the most pitiful. Confined in the great water all day long, they will get sick even if they avoid drowning, eating tree bark, biting grass roots, selling wives and daughters, selling children and grandchildren, these are all. Especially bitter to think about survival, crying on the street, even harder to hear, crying and complaining, touching people's hearts, really different tragic sounds, saying, ladies and gentlemen, lords, have mercy on me. The disaster victims have nowhere to run, I am. Returning home and not seeing my parents' faces, going out and not being able to control the high and low roads, a penny will not fall into the empty space, it will be born in the dark while living in the light, as the saying goes. Good deeds will be rewarded, the heavens will not disappoint good-hearted people, great yin merit is repairing bridges, repairing roads, and repairing temples, small yin merit is giving clothes, giving rice, and giving money, open the golden dragon hand, and live to be one hundred and something, honestly donating foreign money, dripping and rolling, your sons and grandsons will be commanders for generations, bless your hands and feet to be light and healthy without disaster, more blessings, more longevity, more children and grandchildren, officials will be easy to be long and become big, four seasons a year without any sickness, what's more. Donate a little foreign money, a small fresh experience, I hope you will win the aviation ticket every period, trade in gold every day, the real business is really developed, earn gold in the morning and earn silver at night, earn gold in the morning to become tens of millions, earn silver at night to use a bucket, burn incense must burn in a dead temple, saving people must save the disaster victims, I am. Suffering in this life for the sins of my previous life, more bitter than Coptis chinensis, big boss, big sir, everyone is blessed, ah, please show your compassion, save me, a person in distress, think of the disaster victims, not always coming and going, always annoying, but also teaching no way to seek help, ah, there are old clothes, old quilts, old shoes and socks, wearing them can also avoid the cold, temporarily pass through three winters and one spring, good lady, save my life, Yin Gongji's soft-hearted people, donate a little silver money with a good conscience, saving the disaster victims' lives, better than burning incense in the South China Sea, today donating money to save the disaster victims, tomorrow you will have happy thoughts, I hope you, choose a lover who suits your heart, think of them, calling for help on the streets all day long, eating the wind and sleeping in the rain, spending their remaining lives, it is really the eighteenth hell on earth.

Suzhou New Book 188

Yang Zhile's "Taiping Flower"

Dun Ben (800) 3:45 PM to 4:30 PM

Chapter 1: Killing a Chicken to Entertain Guests, Night Talk of Soldiers in a Rural Home

Han Xiaomei delivered the silver lamp to the door of the study. She secretly thought that there were distant guests today. She slowed her lotus steps and looked inside. She saw Han Leyu and Li Shoubai sitting in front of the window, talking and laughing. She deliberately avoided showing her face and placed the lamp on the table inside. She stepped back and gave Shoubai a quick glance, a young gentleman who was very elegant. She couldn't help but admire him privately. Han Leyu was about to call Xiaomei to perform the first meeting ceremony. Xiaomei suddenly thought about preparing dinner in the kitchen and returned from the study. She looked in the kitchen. Apart from the usual home-cooked dishes, there was nothing special to entertain the guests. As she was thinking, she suddenly heard a rooster crowing. This rooster had a tall crown, a majestic appearance, and beautiful feathers, and it was Han Leyu's favorite thing in his life. Because Xiaomei had no special ingredients, she instructed Er Tu to slaughter it to entertain the honored guests.

Movie News

Hu Ping Will Return to Hunan 191

"Hero of the Times" to Start Filming Early

Hu Ping was sick for a while some time ago. Although her plump apple-colored face was a little thinner, her beauty did not diminish in the slightest.

According to Hu Ping herself: "The origin of my illness this time is nothing more than overwork, because I was filming 'Hero of the Times' directed by Ying Yunwei at Yihua, and I had to go to Xinhua to film 'The Peach Blossom Fan' at the same time. Sometimes I was filming day and night, and I didn't have enough rest, which led to the illness." Indeed, it is hard enough to film in this hot weather.

Hu Ping is from Hunan. She left her hometown and her beloved parents to come to this Shanghai, thousands of miles away, to be a soldier in Chinese film culture. It has been more than three years. In these three years, Hu Ping has always wanted to return to her hometown once to see her dear parents, but her ideal has never been realized.

Recently, her father came to Shanghai to see her, not fearing the arduous journey. When the father and daughter, who had been separated for more than three years, met, you can imagine what a moving scene it was, full of both sadness and joy!

Her father told her that her mother's old illness had relapsed and was extremely dangerous. She missed her all day long. Hu Ping's heart was shattered when she heard about her mother's condition, and tears couldn't help but fall down.

Now, Hu Ping has decided to ask Yihua Film Company for a month's leave to return to Hunan to visit her mother. The trip will be in about two weeks. As for the unfinished scenes in "Hero of the Times," she has obtained the consent of director Ying Yunwei to start filming early.

Xinhua Film Company's production of "The Peach Blossom Fan" had a guessing game. Some called it a drunken signature. Jin Yan smiled at it. Hu Ping's handwriting was extremely charming, while Ouyang's handwriting was strong and vigorous. Others, such as Zhang Zhiyun's magnificence and Tong Yuejuan's generosity, were all regarded as treasures by those who obtained them. Others, such as Dai Yanwan, Gu Menghu, Zhang Zhizhi, Zhou Fengwen, and Zha Tianying, each signed hundreds of them and were very busy.
